	<meta property="og:description" content="Green dragons are the weakest of the adult chromatic dragons in RuneScape. They are found in various locations within the Wilderness as well as in the Corsair Cove Dungeon. Green dragons are capable of breathing dragonfire, which can hit up to 50 damage on players who are not wielding an Anti-dragon shield or Dragonfire shield. Using one of these shields will partially block the dragonfire, and using one of these shields with an antifire potion or Protect from Magic will block the dragonfire..." />

</script>

<p><b>Green dragons</b> are the weakest of the adult <a href="/wiki/Chromatic_dragons" title="Chromatic dragons">chromatic dragons</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/RuneScape" title="RuneScape" class="mw-redirect">RuneScape</a></i>. They are found in various locations within the <a href="/wiki/Wilderness" title="Wilderness">Wilderness</a> as well as in the <a href="/wiki/Corsair_Cove_Dungeon" title="Corsair Cove Dungeon">Corsair Cove Dungeon</a>. Green dragons are capable of breathing <a href="/wiki/Dragonfire" title="Dragonfire">dragonfire</a>, which can hit up to 50 damage on players who are not wielding an <a href="/wiki/Anti-dragon_shield" title="Anti-dragon shield">Anti-dragon shield</a> or <a href="/wiki/Dragonfire_shield" title="Dragonfire shield">Dragonfire shield</a>. Using one of these shields will partially block the dragonfire, and using one of these shields with an <a href="/wiki/Antifire_potion" title="Antifire potion">antifire potion</a> or <a href="/wiki/Protect_from_Magic" title="Protect from Magic">Protect from Magic</a> will block the dragonfire completely.  
</p><p>Green dragons are assignable as a <a href="/wiki/Slayer_assignment" title="Slayer assignment">Slayer assignment</a> by <a href="/wiki/Vannaka" title="Vannaka">Vannaka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chaeldar" title="Chaeldar">Chaeldar</a> and <a href="/wiki/Krystilia" title="Krystilia">Krystilia</a>. If players wish to avoid the <a href="/wiki/Risks" title="Risks" class="mw-redirect">risks</a> of the Wilderness when assigned green dragons as a Slayer task, either <a href="/wiki/Baby_dragon_(green)" title="Baby dragon (green)">baby green dragons</a> within the <a href="/wiki/Brimhaven_Dungeon" title="Brimhaven Dungeon">Brimhaven Dungeon</a> can be killed as an alternative or those in the <a href="/wiki/Myths%27_Guild" title="Myths' Guild">Myths' Guild</a> basement. If players want to challenge themselves, <a href="/wiki/Brutal_green_dragon" title="Brutal green dragon">brutal green dragons</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Ancient_Cavern" title="Ancient Cavern">Ancient Cavern</a> can be killed instead.
</p><p><b><span style="color:red">Warning:</span></b> Wilderness locations where green dragons roam are frequently visited by <a href="/wiki/Player-killer" title="Player-killer" class="mw-redirect">player-killers</a>. If you intend on hunting green dragons, an emergency <a href="/wiki/Teleport" title="Teleport" class="mw-redirect">teleport</a>, high healing <a href="/wiki/Food" title="Food">food</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prayer_potion" title="Prayer potion">prayer potions</a> are highly recommended in the event that you are attacked by a player-killer.
</p>
